# big-code-strata-refac-001: Rename FxVanillaOption to FxEuropeanOption in OpenGamma Strata

## Task

Rename the `FxVanillaOption` type family to `FxEuropeanOption` throughout the OpenGamma Strata codebase. The `FxVanillaOption` class in `modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOption.java` represents a European-exercise FX option, but the name "vanilla" is ambiguous. Rename it to `FxEuropeanOption` to clearly communicate the exercise style.

The refactoring includes:
1. Rename 4 core Joda-Beans classes: `FxVanillaOption` → `FxEuropeanOption`, `FxVanillaOptionTrade` → `FxEuropeanOptionTrade`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` → `ResolvedFxEuropeanOption`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` → `ResolvedFxEuropeanOptionTrade`
2. Rename 4 pricer classes: `BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer` → `BlackFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer`, etc.
3. Rename 4 measure classes: `FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations` → `FxEuropeanOptionMeasureCalculations`, etc.
4. Rename the loader plugin: `FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin` → `FxEuropeanOptionTradeCsvPlugin`
5. Update the `ProductType.FX_VANILLA_OPTION` constant and its string value
6. Update all dependent files: `FxSingleBarrierOption` (wraps `FxVanillaOption`), barrier pricers, CSV utilities, trade resolvers
7. Update Joda-Beans auto-generated Meta/Builder inner classes in all renamed files

## Context

- **Repository**: OpenGamma/Strata (Java, ~500K LOC)
- **Category**: Cross-File Refactoring
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: modules/product/fxopt, modules/pricer/fxopt, modules/measure/fxopt, modules/loader/csv

## Requirements

1. Identify ALL files that need modification for this refactoring
2. Document the complete dependency chain showing why each file is affected
3. Implement the changes (or describe them precisely if the scope is too large)
4. Verify that no references to the old API/name remain

...

The\n * option is European, exercised only on the exercise date.\n * <p>\n * For example, a call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange is the option to perform a foreign exchange on the expiry\n *   * the long party, potentially enter into the inverse transaction.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LongShort longShort;\n  /**\n   * The expiry date of the @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final FxSingle underlying;\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an equivalent {@code FxVanillaOption} using currency pair, option expiry, call/put flag, strike, base\n   * currency notional, and underlying payment date.\n   * <p>\n   * No payment date adjustments apply.\n   *\n   * @param longShort the long/short flag of the option\n   * @param expiry notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n   */\n  public static option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n   */\n  public static FxVanillaOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate,\n      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n    CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n    FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxVanillaOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @ImmutableValidator\n  private void validate() {\n    inOrderOrEqual(expiryDate, underlying.getPaymentDate(), \"expiryDate\", \"underlying.paymentDate\");\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  /**\n   * Gets currency pair of the base currency and counter currency.\n   * <p>\n   * This currency pair is * @return the expiry date and time\n   */\n  @Override\n  public ZonedDateTime getExpiry() {\n    return expiryDate.atTime(expiryTime).atZone(expiryZone);\n  }\n\n //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the FX barrier option product.\n   * <p>\n   * The present value of the product is the value on the valuation date.\n   * It is expressed in the counter currency.\n   * <p>\n   * The volatility used in this computation is the Black implied volatility at expiry time and strike.\n   * \n   * @param option  the option product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param volatilities  the Black volatility provider\n   * @return the present value of the product\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    double price = price(option, ratesProvider, volatilities);\n    ResolvedFxEuropeanOption underlyingOption = option.getUnderlyingOption();\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(underlyingOption.getCounterCurrency(), signedNotional(underlyingOption) * price);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price of the FX barrier option product.\n   * <p>\n   * The price of the product is the value on the valuation date for one unit of the base currency \n   * and is expressed in the counter currency. The price does not take into account the long/short flag.\n   * See {@link #presentValue} for scaling and currency.\n   * <p>\n   * The volatility used in this computation is the Black implied volatility at expiry time and strike.\n   * \n   * @param option  the option product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param volatilities  the Black volatility provider\n   * @return the price of the product\n   */\n  public double price(\n      ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    validate(option, ratesProvider, volatilities);\n    SimpleConstantContinuousBarrier barrier = (SimpleConstantContinuousBarrier) option.getBarrier();\n    ResolvedFxEuropeanOption underlyingOption = option.getUnderlyingOption();\n    double timeToExpiry = volatilities.relativeTime(underlyingOption.getExpiry());\n    if (timeToExpiry < 0d) {\n      return 0d;\n    }\n    ResolvedFxSingle underlyingFx = underlyingOption.getUnderlying();\n    CurrencyPair currencyPair = underlyingFx.getCurrencyPair();\n    double todayFx = ratesProvider.fxRate(currencyPair);\n    Currency ccyBase = underlyingFx.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency();\n    Currency ccyCounter = underlyingFx.getCounterCurrencyPayment().getCurrency();\n    if (alreadyTouched(todayFx, barrier)) {\n      if (barrier.getKnockType().isKnockIn()) {\n        return VANILLA_OPTION_PRICER.price(underlyingOption, ratesProvider, volatilities);\n      } else if (option.getRebate().isPresent()) {\n        CurrencyAmount rebate = option.getRebate().get();\n        DaysAdjustment spotLag = spotAdjustment(currencyPair);\n        LocalDate paymentDate = spotLag.adjust(ratesProvider.getValuationDate(), ReferenceData.standard());\n        double rebatePrice = rebate.getAmount() * ratesProvider.discountFactor(rebate.getCurrency(), paymentDate) /\n            Math.abs(underlyingFx.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getAmount());\n        return rebate.getCurrency().equals(ccyCounter) ? rebatePrice : todayFx * rebatePrice;\n      }\n      return 0d;\n    }\n    DiscountFactors baseDiscountFactors = ratesProvider.discountFactors(ccyBase);\n    DiscountFactors counterDiscountFactors = ratesProvider.discountFactors(ccyCounter);\n    double rateBase = baseDiscountFactors.zeroRate(underlyingFx.getPaymentDate());\n    double rateCounter = counterDiscountFactors.zeroRate(underlyingFx.getPaymentDate());\n    double costOfCarry = rateCounter - rateBase;\n    double dfBase = baseDiscountFactors.discountFactor(underlyingFx.getPaymentDate());\n    double dfCounter = counterDiscountFactors.discountFactor(underlyingFx.getPaymentDate());\n    double strike = underlyingOption.getStrike();\n    double forward = todayFx * dfBase / dfCounter;\n    double volatility = volatilities.volatility(currencyPair, underlyingOption.getExpiry(), strike, forward);\n    double price = BARRIER_PRICER.price(\n        todayFx, strike, timeToExpiry, costOfCarry, rateCounter, volatility, underlyingOption.getPutCall().isCall(), barrier);\n    if (option.getRebate().isPresent()) {\n      CurrencyAmount rebate = option.getRebate().get();\n      double priceRebate = rebate.getCurrency().equals(ccyCounter) ?\n          CASH_REBATE_PRICER.price(todayFx, timeToExpiry, costOfCarry, rateCounter, volatility, barrier.inverseKnockType()) :\n          ASSET_REBATE_PRICER.price(todayFx, timeToExpiry, costOfCarry, rateCounter, volatility, barrier.inverseKnockType());\n      price += priceRebate * rebate.getAmount() / Math.abs(underlyingFx.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getAmount());\n    }\n    return price;\n  }\n\n sensitivity of the product is the sensitivity of {@link #presentValue} to\n   * the underlying curves.\n   * <p>\n   * The volatility is fixed in this sensitivity computation, i.e., sticky-strike.\n   * \n   * @param option  the option product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param volatilities  the Black volatility provider\n   * @return the present value curve sensitivity of BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    ResolvedFxEuropeanOption underlyingOption = option.getUnderlyingOption();\n    double timeToExpiry = volatilities.relativeTime(underlyingOption.getExpiry());\n    if (timeToExpiry <= 0d) {\n      return PointSensitivityBuilder.none();\n    }\n    SimpleConstantContinuousBarrier barrier = # FxVanillaOption to FxEuropeanOption Refactoring

## Summary
Complete refactoring to rename the `FxVanillaOption` type family to `FxEuropeanOption` throughout the OpenGamma Strata codebase (49 files across 5 modules).

## Files Examined and Modified

### Core Product Classes (4 files renamed + 4 test files)
- **modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOption.java** → FxEuropeanOption.java
  - Main Joda Bean class representing a European-exercise FX option
  - Class renamed: FxVanillaOption → FxEuropeanOption
  - Inner classes: FxEuropeanOption.Meta, FxEuropeanOption.Builder

- **modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTrade.java** → FxEuropeanOptionTrade.java
  - Trade wrapper for FxEuropeanOption
  - Class renamed: FxVanillaOptionTrade → FxEuropeanOptionTrade
  - References FxEuropeanOption (renamed dependency)

- **modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOption.java** → ResolvedFxEuropeanOption.java
  - Resolved form of FxEuropeanOption
  - Class renamed: ResolvedFxVanillaOption → ResolvedFxEuropeanOption
  - Joda Bean with auto-generated Meta/Builder classes

- **modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade.java** → ResolvedFxEuropeanOptionTrade.java
  - Resolved form of FxEuropeanOptionTrade
  - Class renamed: ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade → ResolvedFxEuropeanOptionTrade
  - References ResolvedFxEuropeanOption

- **Test files** (4): FxVanillaOptionTest.java, FxVanillaOptionTradeTest.java, ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTest.java, ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTradeTest.java

### Pricer Classes (8 files + 4 test files)

#!/bin/bash
# Refactoring script: FxVanillaOption -> FxEuropeanOption

cd /workspace

echo "========== STEP 1: Rename core product files =========="
mv modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOption.java \
   modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxEuropeanOption.java

mv modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTrade.java \
   modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxEuropeanOptionTrade.java

mv modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOption.java \
   modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxEuropeanOption.java

   modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxEuropeanOptionTrade.java
